 aaj apana 40waan janmdin manaa rahe tendulkar narayan kii sidhi gend ko chookkar bold hue jabaki karthik ko sachitr senanayake ne pagabaadha out kiya
 Smith completed his first half-century of IPL six in just 34 balls with two runs after scoring four and six off Senanayake's consecutive balls
 smith ke tufaan ke bich gambhir ne gend apane star spinner narayan ko thamai jinhone captain ko niraash nahin karte hue apane is hamatvan ballebaaj ko sthanapann khilaadi brandan maikulam ke haathon kaich kara diya
 Captain Rohit then took the front
 unhone senanayake par do chakke jadkar apane tevar dikhaae
 KKR needed 44 runs to win the final five overs
 rohit or pollard ne team ko lakshya ke kareeb pahunchaaya lekin narayan ne mumbai ke captain ko apni hi gend par lapak liya
 Pollard hit a six over Senanayake but when the team needed 10 runs to win in the final over, he was caught by Rajat Bhatia off Manoj Tiwary
 unhone 24 gend kii apni pari main do chauke or ek chakka maaraa
 Harbhajan Singh (07 not out) was followed by a six over Bhatia and Ambati Rayudu (13 not out) ensured the team's victory
 isse pehle kolkata ke ballebaaj acchhee shuruyaat ko badi pari main badalane main naakaam rahe
 Jacques Kallis top scored with 37 while Tiwary contributed 33 and Eoin Morgan contributed 31 runs
 tiwari or morgan ne chauthe wicket ke liye 6
 Also added 54 runs in 2 overs
 barish ke kaaran match aadha ghanta der se shuru hua
 Kolkata captain Gambhir and Yusuf Pathan (19) hit 26 runs in the first over of Harbhajan's innings
 pathan ne harbhajan kii pehali chaar gendon par teen chauke or ek chakka maaraa jabaki gambhir ne bhi is aaf spinner par chakka jadaa
 Pathan, however, could not continue his stance and in the next over, Mitchell Johnson caught Harbhajan in the slip
 gambhir or jaak kallis ne iske baad pari ko aage badhaayaa
 Kallis hit two boundaries in Malinga's over
 donon ne chah over main team kaa score ek wicket par 61 ran tak pahunchaaya
 However, when Gambhir looked in good touch, Ojha played the ball in the air in an attempt to move the ball forward and Harbhajan made a mistake in catching it in the cover
 gambhir ne 20 gend main do chaukon or ek chakke kii madad se 26 ran banaae
 Kallis got a life on the ball off Ojha on a personal score of 22 but he failed to take advantage of this and the left-arm spinner caught Rohit in the cover in the next over and returned to the pavilion
 unhone 38 gend kii apni pari main chaar chauke maare
 The comments team ko bade score tak pahunchane kii jimmedaari ab tiwari or morgan par thi
 After opening the account with fours on leg-spinner Yuzvendra Chahal, Tiwari sent his consecutive balls for fours and sixes
 morgan ne bhi is leg spinner par chaukaa jadaa
 Morgan hit a four and a six off Johnson's consecutive balls in the 18th over but caught Rohit in the next ball
 malinga ne pari ke antim over main sirf teen ran die or tiwari or devabrata das (06) ko bold kiya
 KKR added 47 runs in the final five overs
 smith ne senanayake kii lagaataar gendon par chaukaa or chakka jadne ke baad do ran ke saath sirf 34 gend main ipel chah kaa apana pehla ardhshtak puraa kiya
 Amidst the storm of Smith, Gambhir held the ball to his star spinner Narayan, who did not disappoint the captain and caught his fellow batsman at the hands of substitute Brandon mccullum
 captain rohit ne iske baad morcha sambhala

 keker ko antim paanch over main jeet ke liye 44 ran kii darkaar thi

 pollard ne senanayake par chakka jadaa lekin team ko antim over main jeet ke liye jab 10 ran chahie the jab vah rajat bhaatia kii gend par manoj tiwari ko kaich de baithe
 He hit two fours and a six in his 24-ball innings
 harbhajan singh (naabad 07) ne iske baad bhaatia par chakka or ambati rayudu (naabad 13) ne chaukaa jadkar team kii jeet sunishchit kii
 Earlier, Kolkata batsmen failed to convert a good start into a big innings
 jaak kallis ne sarvaadhik 37 ran kii pari kheli jabaki tiwari ne 33 or eon morgan ne 31 ran kaa yogadan diya
 Tiwary and Morgan scored 6 for the fourth wicket
 2 over main 54 ran kii saajhedaari bhi kii
 The match started half an hour late due to rain
 kolkata ke captain gambhir or yusuf pathan (19) ne harbhajan ke pari ke pehle over main hi 26 ran thok daale
 Pathan hit three fours and a six off Harbhajan's first four balls while Gambhir also hit a six off the off-spinner
 pathan haalanki apane tevar aage jari nahin rakh paae or agle over main mishael janson kii gend par slip main harbhajan ko kaich de baithe
 Gambhir and Jacques Kallis then led the innings
 kallis ne malinga ke over main do chauke jade
 Both of them reached 61 for one wicket in six overs
 gambhir haalanki jab acchhee lay main dikh rahe the tab ojha kii gend ko aage badhkar khilne kii koshish main gend ko hawa main khel gaye or harbhajan ne cover main ise lapakane main koi galati kii
 Gambhir scored 26 runs in 20 balls with the help of two fours and a six
 kallis ko 22 ran ke nijee score par ojha kii gend par jeevandaan mila lekin vah iskaa phayda uthaane main naakaam rahe or baayen haath ke is spinner ke agle over main cover main rohit ko kaich dekar pavilion laut gaye

 tippaniyan The responsibility for the team to reach the big score was now on Tiwary and Morgan

 Morgan also hit a four on this leg-spinner
 morgan ne 18wein over main janson kii lagaataar gendon par chaukaa or chakka jadaa lekin agali gend main rohit ko kaich de baithe
 Malinga conceded just three runs in the final over of the innings and bowled Tiwari and Devabrata Das (06)
 keker ne antim paanch over main 47 ran jode
